Treat your classmates as you would have them treat you.   
③3 He who can say a great deal in a few words is a master of speaking.   
By studying our breathing we learn that we take only a small amount of air into our lungs each time that we breathe.   
The snowstorm was so severe that all trains were delayed.   
The boys marched just as trained soldiers do.   
He who reaps must first sow.   
Make a note of the assignment lest you forget it.   
I solved as many of the problems as I could.   
Have you heard about who the new teacher is and when she will come?

# (三十三)

# 从句联词的省略

联词 that 可省去，引导从句宾/表语[1]。

限定定语从句前， 有些联词也省去：

联词若是宾/状/表，成分作用在从句；

联词之前有介词， 联词省去、介后移[2]。

从句用在口语中， 省去联词有几例：

句首 Any/It/Who, 谓语 here/there be;

主句带有 such/so, that 说明结果时[3]。

# 说明：

[1] 用 that 做联词的宾语或表语从句，可以把 that 省去，如：

1）He said (that) he could come. (宾语从句)

他说他能来。

2) The trouble is (that) he will not agree. (表语从句)

难办的是他会不同意。

[2] 限定性定语从句的联词也有一些是可以省去的：

1）联词是从句的宾语，如：

Do you know the people (whom) we met at the gate?

你认识我们在门口遇到的那个人吗？

2）联词是从句的状语，如：

This is the reason(why)he has done like that.

这就是他那样做的理由。

注意：限定性定语从句的引导词where不能省略，如：

This is the city where I lived.

这就是我住过的那个城市。

3）联词是从句的表语，如：

He is not the man (that) he used to be.

他不是过去那样的人了。

4）联词前有介词时，可以省去联词，把介词移到从句的谓语动词之后，如：

Air will completely fill any container in which it may be placed.

=Air will completely fill any container(which) it may be placed in.

空气可以充满任何能够容纳它的容器。

[3] 在口语中，句子的开头是 Any/It/Who，或者不论在主句或从句中有 here be 或 there be 做谓语时，限定性定语从句的联词常被省略。另外，主句带有 such 或 so，后加说明结果的状语从句，则联词 that 也可省去。例如：

(1) It is not everyone (who/that) can get such a chance like this.

不是每个人都能得到这样的机会。

(2) Who was that (who/that)telephoned a moment ago?

刚才打电话的人是谁？

(3) Anyone (who/that) does that ought to be punished.

谁那样做都应该受到惩罚。

(4) Jack doesn't smoke ordinary marijuana, he uses the highest quality stuff (that) there is.

杰克不吸一般的大麻，而是用质量最高的。

(5) There is something (that) I want to say. 我有事要说。

(6) Here is a book (that/which) will tell you how to play tennis.

这儿有一本教你怎样打网球的书。

(7) It is such a good chance (that) we mustn't miss it.

这是一个我们一定不能失掉的好机会。

(8) He was so nervous (that) he made a lot of mistakes.

他是如此紧张，以致出了很多错误。

# 练习（33）

括号中的联词是可以省去的，说明为什么：

1 Have you read the novel (which) I lent you last week?   
$②$ Helium is a gas(which) we obtain from the air.   
$③$ I know (that) you have made great success in your

experiment.

The room (which) I stayed in was dark and gloomy.   
$⑤$ I didn't know the material (which) this tool is made of.   
$⑥$ This is the reason(why) he wants to do this.   
There was somebody(who) wanted to see you.   
$⑧$ Who is that (whom) you are going to see?   
It is the problem (that) must be explained.   
The moment(when)he entered the room, I found he was tired.   
This is the room (which) they held the meeting in.   
The truth is (that) I don't really know myself.   
He was so massive (that) the room seemed to shrink.   
Here is a notice (that) will tell you a good news.   
$⑤$ Anybody(who)works harder will get more.   
He is not the man (that) he was.

# （三十四）

# 直接引语变间接引语

<table><tr><td>直接引语是原话，</td><td>间接引语述其意，</td></tr><tr><td>去掉引号变从句，</td><td>或是变成不定式：</td></tr><tr><td>从句 that 做引导，</td><td>原话本是陈述句；</td></tr><tr><td>if/whether 做联词，</td><td>原话一般疑问句；</td></tr><tr><td>疑问词做联词时，</td><td>原话特殊疑问句；</td></tr><tr><td>直接引语是祈使，</td><td>间接引语不定式[1]。</td></tr><tr><td>直接引语变间接，</td><td>代词变化要合理[2]。</td></tr><tr><td>注意从句变时态，</td><td>主句谓语做依据：</td></tr><tr><td>现在/将来/完成时，</td><td>从句时态照原句[3]；</td></tr><tr><td>主句谓语是过去，</td><td>相应过去变从句[4]；</td></tr><tr><td>所说情况永不变，</td><td>从句总是现在时[5]。</td></tr><tr><td>此外还有一些词，</td><td>要随时态做变易[6]。</td></tr></table>

# 说明：

[1] 直接引语（the direct quotation）是引用的原话，要加上引号。间接引语（the indirect quotation）不是原话，而是重述原话的大意。直接引语变为间接引语的方式有四种：

1）原话是陈述句（包括肯定和否定），间接引语是用that

（可以省去）引导的从句，如：

(1) He said, "I have seen the film."

他说：“我看过这部电影。”

—He said (that) he had seen the film.

他说他看过这部电影。

He said, "I haven't seen the film."

他说：“我没有看过这部电影。”

—He said (that) he hadn't seen the film.

他说他没有看过这部电影。

2）直接引语是一般疑问句，间接引语变为用if/whether（是不是）做联词的从句。主句原来的动词，如果是say，要变为ask（问）/want to know（想知道）/wonder（不知道）/…等。例如：

① He said, "May I use the bike?"

他说：“我可以用这辆自行车吗？”

He asked if (whether) he could use the bike.

他问他是否可以用这辆自行车。

② He said, “Have you seen the film?”

他说：“你看过这部电影吗？”

He asked if (whether) she had seen the film.

他问她是否看过这部电影。

3）直接引语是特殊疑问句（用疑问词Who/What/When/Where/How/Why/…开头的疑问句），变为间接引语时，从句仍然是以原来的疑问词开头，但要注意：后边跟随的是一个陈述句。原来的主句动词，如果是say，要变为ask/inquire(问)/…之类的动词。

例如：

① He said, "What have you done?"

他说：“你干什么来着？”

—He asked what he had done.

他问他干什么来着。

He asked, "What is her name?"

他问：“她叫什么名字？”

He asked what her name was.

他问她的名字叫什么。

4）直接引语是祈使句，变为间接引语时，要把原来的话变为不定式。主句的动词，如果原来是say，要变为tell叫/ask(request)要求/order command)命令/之类的动词。例如：

He said, "Do more practice, students."

他说：“同学们要多做练习。”

—He told the students to do more practice. 他叫学生们多做练习。

[2] 直接引语变为从句做间接引语时，从句的代词要做合理的变化，如：

1) He said, "I want this."

他说：“我想要这个。”

—He said (that) he wanted that.

他说他想要那一个。

2) He said to me, "Do you know?"

他对我说：“你知道吗？”

—He asked me if I knew.

他问我是否知道。

[3] 直接引语的主句谓语时态是一般现在时、一般将来时或现在完成时，间接引语从句动词的时态照原来直接引语的时态不变，如：

1) He often says, "I like sports."

他常说：“我爱好体育活动。”

He often says (that) he likes sports.

他常说他爱好体育活动。

2) He has said, "I'll come."

他刚才说：“我要来。”

—He has said (that) he'll come.

他刚才说过他要来。

3) He will say, "I've read the novel."

他会说：“我看过这部小说。”

—He will say (that) he's read the novel.

他会说他看过这部小说。

[4] 主句的谓语时态是过去式，间接引语从句动词的时态就要按照原来的时态变为相应的过去形式，如：

He said, "I have been there."

他说：“我去过那里。”

—He said (that) he had been there. 他说他去过那里。注意：主句的动词是过去式，间接引语从句动词的相应变化是：

$①$ 一般现在 $\longrightarrow$ 一般过去  
② 现在进行 $\longrightarrow$ 过去进行  
$⑧$ 一般过去 $④$ 现在完成 $\rightarrow$ 过去完成 $⑤$ 过去完成

⑥ 过去进行 $\rightarrow$ 过去完成进行  
⑦ 一般将来 $\longrightarrow$ 过去将来

[5] 如果所说的情况是永远不变的，无论主句的动词是什么时态，从句也要用一般现在时，如：

He said, "The sun rises in the east."

他说过：“太阳是从东方升起的。”

—He said (that) the sun rises in the east.

他说过太阳是从东方升起的。

[6] 另外还有一些词也要随着间接引语时态的改变，相应地加以变化，如：

1) this $\rightarrow$ that   
2) these→those   
3) here $\longrightarrow$ there   
4) today--that day   
5) yesterday- $\rightarrow$ the day before   
6) tomorrow $\rightarrow$ the next (following) day   
7) next year (month/week/term/…等)→the next (following)year (month/week/term/…等)   
8) last year (month/week/term/…等)→the previous year (month/week/term/…等)

# 附注：

1. 当直接引语的一般过去时需要变为过去完成时的时候，如果有具体的时间状语，就还要用一般过去时，如：

The teacher said, "Columbus discovered America in 1492."

老师说过：“哥伦布在1492年发现了美洲。”

—The teacher said (that) Columbus discovered America in 1492.

老师说过哥伦布在1492年发现了美洲。

2. 直接引语的主句（如…said）可以放在直接引语之前或之后，也可以放在中间。主句放在中间或后边时都可以用倒装句。但是变为间接引语时，一律要把主句放在作为从句的间接引语之前，不能倒装。例如：

(1) Jane said, "I am glad to see you."

珍说：“高兴见到你。”

Jane said (that) she was glad to see him.

珍说高兴见到他。

(2) "We have moved in our new home." Ruth told me.

露斯告诉我：“我们已搬进了新居。”

—Ruth told me (that) they had moved in their new home.

露斯告诉我他们已搬进了新居。

(3) "This canary," said the seller (the seller said), "is a good singer."

卖主说：“这只金丝雀是个好歌手。”

The seller said (that) that canary was a good singer.

卖主说那只金丝雀是个好歌手。

3. 各种形式混合的直接引语变为间接引语时，可以采用并列的形式，如：

He said, "Did you hear that crash? Go and see what happened."

他说：“你听到撞击声了吗？去看看出了什么事。”

He asked if she had heard that crash and told her to go and see what had happened.

他问她是否听到了撞击声，叫她去看看出了什么事。

# 练习 (34)

将下列各句的直接引语变为间接引语：

① He said, "I have lost my umbrella."   
He says, "The train will be late."   
$③$ He said, "She is working in the garden."   
He says, "I shall be there."   
He said, "I have bought a typewriter."   
⑥ He said, "I like this one."   
They said, "We are going back to our own country."   
He said, "There are countless stars in the Milky Way galaxy."   
He says, "Where do you live?"   
He said, "Where is the station?"   
① "What is your name?" he said to her.   
He inquired, "Was anyone here yesterday?"   
"Will he come if it rains?" she wondered.   
He said, "Was she born in 1914?"   
He said, "Get your coat mended, Tom."   
He says, "Don't move, boys."   
She said, "Shut the door after you, children."   
"I shall tell you a story tonight," my aunt promised.

19 "How many problems have you solved?" asked Fred.   
She said, "I like this very much."   
He asked, "How long have you been there?"   
He said, "These books are new."   
He said, "He will come today."   
He said, "I shall complete this experiment next year."   
He said, "I met him last week."   
He said, "I am reading a very interesting novel."   
He said, "Where were you last year."   
He said, "It rained yesterday."   
He said, "Mary looks terrible. Is she ill?"   
He said, "I don't know the way. Ask the old man over there."

# (三十五)

# It 在句子中的作用

代词 it 译成“它”， “这、那”等等都可以。

有时指的是时间， 或指天气或距离[2]。

也许本身无意义， 当作主、宾是形式。

that 或 who 从句前，强调语气 It be[4]。

# 说明：

[1] it 这个代词, 除了译成“它”之外, 也可以译成“这、那”等等, 如:

1) It is a kitten.

它是一只小猫。

2) It is a fine day.

这是一个好天气。

3) It is very good.

那很好。

[2] it 可以用来指时间/天气/距离/…等，如：

It is seven now.

现在，时间是七点钟。

2) It is very cold.

天气很冷。

3) It is very far.

距离很远。

[3] 如果句子的主语或宾语比较长（一般是从句或非谓语动词词组），可以把it放在主语或宾语的位置，把真正的主语或宾语移到句后去，it没有意义，作为形式上的主语或宾语，如：

1）It is necessary to make a plan. 主（形式）谓 表 主（不定式）↑

做个计划是必要的。

2）It is no use only talking. 主（形式）谓 表 主（动名词）

光说是没有用的。

3）It is regrettable that he did not see the film. 主（形式）谓 表 主（从句）

他没有看这部电影是遗憾的。

4) He felt it difficult to do this work. 主谓 宾（形式） 宾补 实（不定式）

他觉得这项工作做起来有困难。

5) I think it no use advising him. 主谓 宾(形式) 宾补 宾(动名词)

我认为劝告他是没有用的。

6) We have made it clear that agriculture is the 主 谓 宾（从句） 1 foundation of the national economy.

我们已经明确农业是国民经济的基础。

[4] 用 It be + 被强调部分（主、宾、状或介宾）+ that/who 引导的从句构成强调语气句，如：

1) It is you who helped me.

被强调部分（主）

是你帮助了我。

2) It was yesterday that we held a class meeting.

被强调部分（状）

是昨天，我们开了一个班会。

3) It is because the book is useful that I bought it.

被强调部分（状）

是因为这本书有用，我才买了它。

4) It was in the street that I met him yesterday.

被强调部分（状）

那是在街上，昨天我遇到他。

5) It is the place that we have been wanting to.

被强调部分（宾）

visit.

我们一直想参观的就是这个地方。

6) It is Mr. Chen that I want to call on, not Miss

被强调部分（介宾）

Cheng.

我要见的是陈先生而不是程小姐。

# 附注：

强调语气从句的引导词只能用 that 或 who。只有被强调部分指的是人，从句的引导词才能用 who；that 则可以通用，指人、事、物、地点、时间、方式、原因…都可以。

# 练习（）

说明下列各句中it的作用：

① It is a giraffe.   
② It was a windy day.   
③ It is fine.   
It was in the morning one day.   
⑤ It is a long way.   
It is foolish to waste your time.   
It was cloudy and cold.   
⑧ Is it any use only talking?   
It is regrettable that you believed such a rumour.   
We have made it clear that modernization is necessary to consolidate the socialist system of our country.   
It was in 1976 that an unprecedented earthquake happened.   
It was we who cleaned the yard.   
It was when he was seven that he began to learn to read and write.   
It was in the auditorium that we held a science forum yesterday.   
It is the red book that I want, not the green one.   
It was Harry that I gave the book to, not Jo·n.

# (三十六)

# 简略句

句有简略式， 规律要记清：

回答是与否[1]， 反意提疑问[2]；

句中相同词， 省掉不需重[3]；

as if/as/when, if/though 等从句中，

主语代词谓语be， 有时二者都可省[4]。

分词词组做状语， 词组常常省being[5]。

# 说明：

[1] 对一般疑问句的回答可用简略句，如：

Are you a pupil?

你是学生吗？

Yes, I am.

是，我是。

No, I am not.

不，我不是。

[2] 陈述句后附加的反意疑问句，必须用简略句，如：

You study English, don't you?

你学习英语，不是吗？

[3] 在一句话中，前边已经出现过的词，后边再用到时，可以

省去, 不重复, 如:

1) The weather is warm and the sky (is) bright.

天气是温暖的，天空是晴朗的。

2) You may go with them if you want to (go with them).

你可以和他们一起，要是你想的话。

[4] as if/as/when/if/through/…等所引导的从句，有时可以省去主语和谓语中的be。规律如下：

1）从句的主语是it、谓语中有be时，不论什么情况，都可以把it和be省去，如：

① I will go with you if (it is) possible. 如有可能，我将和你一起去。

② You may use my dictionary when (it is) necessary.

需要时，你可以用我的字典。

③ The night sky, as (it is) seen from the moon, is wonderful.

从月球上来看，夜空是很美的。

2）从句的主语是it以外的其它代词，只有从句和主句是同一个主语时才能省去从句的主语和谓语中的be,如：

① He looks as if (he is) in full confidence. 看起来，他好象是满有信心。

$②$ She is learned though (she is) very young. 她学识渊博，虽然她很年轻。

[5] 由分词 being 构成的词组做状语时，可以把 being 省去，只保留它的表语部分，如：

1) Being anxious for a quick decision the chairman called for a vote.

=Anxious for a quick decision, the chairman called for a vote.

为求速决，主席提出投票表决。

2) Being too nervous to reply, he stared at the floor.

=Too nervous to reply, he stared at the floor.

由于紧张而不能做出回答，他低下了头发愣。

# 附注：

英语中还有一些不成规律的简略句，只能当作非正式的习惯用语，如：

(1) Nervous, the man opened the letter.

=The man, nervous, opened the letter.   
=The man opened the letter, nervous.   
=The man, who was nervous, opened the letter.

那个人，他很紧张，把信拆开了。

(2) She glanced with disgust at the cat, dead.

=She glanced with disgust at the cat, which was dead.

她厌恶地看了一眼那只猫，那是一只死猫。

(3) Strange how she still likes him.

=It is strange how she still likes him.

奇怪的是她怎么还是喜欢他。

(4) The apples were picked ripe.

=The apples were picked when they were ripe.

这些苹果是熟了才摘的。

(5) Flying through the air at the speed of sound, a sudden thought struck me.

=When the plane flying through the air at the speed of sound, a sudden thought struck me.

当飞机以音速穿空飞行时，一种突然的意念涌现在我的心头。

(6) They toured the college, at one time an institution of high repute.

=They toured the college, which was at one time an institution of high repute.

他们游览了那所学院，那曾经是名噪一时的学府。

(7) Seventy-three people have been drowned in the area, many of them children.

= Seventy-three people have been drowned in the area, many of them being children.

这地方已经淹死过七十三个人，其中很多是小孩。

(8) Think I'll go now.

=I think I'll go now.

我想我现在该走了。

(9) Doesn't look too well.

=He (She) doesn't look too well.

看来他（她）身体不太好。

(10) Must be somebody waiting for you.

=There must be somebody waiting for you.

准是有人在等你。

(11) Afraid not.

=We are afraid not.

恐怕不是吧。

(12) No wonder he's late.

=It is no wonder that he's late.

难怪他来晚。

(13) John done his homework?

=Has John done his homework?

约翰做完作业了吗？

(14) Whatever your problems, they can't worse than mine.

=Whatever your problems are, they can't be worse than mine.

不论你的问题是什么，总不会比我的问题更糟。

# 练习 (36)

去掉下列句子中可以省略的词：

① Some of us study English, others study French.   
② In autumn, the breeze is moderate and the sky is bright.   
$③$ A stream is not wider than a river is wide.   
④ You may come any time if you like to come.   
$⑤$ I will help you when it is necessary.   
⑥ The city, as it is seen from the top of a mountain, is magnificent.   
He is prudent, though he is very young.   
$⑧$ He looks as if he is mad at somebody.   
Have you watched the performance? Yes, I have

wathed the performance.

On the right side of the Ancient Palace is Zhong Shan Park, and on the left side of the Ancient Palace is the Working People's Culture Palace.

# (三十七)

# 倒装句

表、状提到句前去， 主语谓语倒顺序[1]。

谓语动词只一个， 主语代词莫后移[2]；

助词不管有多少， 只到最前留其余[3]。

虚拟语气省 if, 随着前言搭后语,

还有表达祝愿意， 这些都用倒装句[4]。

遇到强调宾语时， 宾语移到句前去[5]。

# 说明：

[1] 为了强调, 句子的表语或状语可以提到句子的开头, 同时主语和谓语的顺序也可以颠倒, 如:

1） So happy are the students. 表 谓 主

学生们是如此地高兴。

（此句的正常顺序是：The students are so happy.）

2) Out rushed the boy. 状 谓 主

那个男孩冲了出去。

（此句的正常顺序是：The boy rushed out.）

[2] 当把句子的表语或状语提到句子的开头时，如果主语是代词，谓语只是一个动词，主语和谓语就不要颠倒顺序，

如：

1) So happy they are. (They are so happy.) 表 主(代) 谓

他们是如此地高兴。

2) Out he rushed. (He rushed out.) 状主（代）谓

他冲了出去。

[3] 谓语如有助动词(包括情态动词)，为了强调而把表语或状语提到句首时，只把谓语中的第一个助动词（或情态动词)提到主语之前，其它不变，如：

1) Never have I seen such a good film. 状 谓(助)主 谓(动) 宾

这么好的电影，我从来没有看过。

（此句的正常顺序是：I have never seen such a good film.）

2) Never so kindly have they been treated.状 谓（助）主 谓（助）谓（动）

这么好的待遇，他们从来没有受到过。

（此句的正常顺序是：They have never been treated so kindly.）

但是，遇到主语较长，又无宾语时，为了避免头重脚轻而把状(表)语和谓语提到主语前的倒装句，其谓语部分要全部移到主语之前，如：

To the payroll must be added the names of the 状 谓 主

new workers.

要新工人的名字加到工资表上去。

（此句的正常顺序是：The names of the new workers must be added to the payroll.)

[4] 不论什么情况，主语和谓语都要颠倒的有以下几种：

1）用if引导的虚拟语气从句，如果省去if，主语和谓语的位置一律要颠倒，如：

Were I you, I would try. (If I were you, I would try.)

我要是你，我就试试看。

2）随着前言搭后语的句子，即接着前边的话来说也如何(So…)或也不如何(Nor(Neither)…)，可以用倒装句，主语和谓语的位置一律要颠倒，如：

$①$ He came early. So did I.(I came early, too.) 状 谓 主

他来得早。我也如此。

You don't know. Nor(Neither)do I. (I don't

know, either.)

你不知道。我也不知道。

注意：前边句子的谓语如有助动词或情态动词，So或Nor(Neither)后边的谓语可以简略到只用一个助动词或情态动词，如：

① You have been there. So have I.

你到那里去过。我也去过。

$②$ He could not complete the task on time. Nor (Neither) could I. 调（情）

他不能按时完成这项任务。我也不能。

3）表示祝愿的句子，常常是用倒装，如：

① Long live the People's Republic of China! 状 谓 主

中华人民共和国万岁！

② May you succeed! 谓(情) 主 谓(动)

祝你成功！

[5] 为了强调、突出，可以把宾语提到主语之前，如：

This book I like very much.

这本书我很喜欢。

# 附注：

1. 直接引语的主句放在引语之后或之间时，可以倒装也可以不倒装，如：

(1) "You may go home now," said the teacher (或 the teacher said).

老师说：“你们现在可以回家了。”

(2) "Teacher," said the monitor (或 the monitor said), "what shall we do this afternoon?"

“老师，”班长说，“今天下午我们干什么？”

2. 用than做联词的比较句，为了强调，than后的主语和谓语也可以颠倒，如：

The seal is even more adapted to an aquatic life than is the otter (=than the otter is adapted to an

acquatic life).

海豹比水獭更适应水中生活。

3. 为了避免词的重复，也可以把并列句改成倒装的比较从句，如：

Harry is usually tall, and his brothers are usually tall.

可以改为：

Harry is usually tall, as are his brothers.

哈里和他的兄弟们都是中等身材。

4. 问或也有这样的倒装句, 如:

(1) They elected as chairman Martin Jones.

$$
= \text {T h e y}
$$

他们选了马丁·琼斯当主席。

(2) Sad though $\mathfrak{H}$ was,

$$
= \text {T h o u g h} I \text {w a s} \text {s a d}, \dots
$$

虽然我悲伤，…

(3) Be that as it may.

$$
= \text {H o w e v e r t h a t m a y b e}.
$$

不管怎么样。

# 练习（37）

将下列句子中的划线部分提前，把原句变为倒装句：

$①$ The weather was terribly hot.   
It is rainy and wet.   
$③$ He went away.   
The stranger left hurriedly.   
The working people work industriously.

$⑥$ I have never heard such a story.   
⑦ I can hardly see the mark.   
The liner was so enormous that it could not enter the harbour.   
If you had worked even harder, you would have succeeded.   
You may be happy!

# (三十八)

# 动词的时态

四种时间各四式， 联想对比便于记。

时间现在和过去，各自还有将来时；

一般、完成、进行式，完成进行是四式[1]。

四四共有十六种， 看来繁杂掌握易；

除去 have/be 以外，动词变化有规律[2]。

说明：

[1] 动词的时态(tenses)变化有四种时间，每种时间又各有四种形式，共为十六种时态。除了have和be以外，动词的时态变化是有固定规律的。以work为例，列表如下：

<table><tr><td>式 时</td><td>一 般</td><td>完 成</td><td>进 行</td><td>完成进行</td></tr><tr><td>现在</td><td>work (原形) works (第三人称单 数)</td><td>have \( \left. \begin{array}{l} \text{ have } \\  \text{ has } \\  \text{ (第三人 } \\  \text{ 称单数) } \end{array}\right\}  \overset{\text{ work- }}{\text{ ed }} \) (过去 分词)</td><td>am is are \( \} \) working (现在分 词)</td><td>have \( \left. \begin{array}{l} \text{ have } \\  \text{ has } \\  \text{ (第三人 } \\  \text{ 称单数) } \end{array}\right\} \) been + work- ing (现在分词)</td></tr><tr><td>过去</td><td>worked (过去式)</td><td>had worked (过去分词)</td><td>was \( \left. \begin{array}{l} \text{ was } \\  \text{ were } \end{array}\right\} \) working (现在分词)</td><td>had been + working (现在分词)</td></tr><tr><td>将来</td><td>shall work(原形)</td><td>shall have + worked (过去分词)</td><td>shall be + working (现在分词)</td><td>shall have will been + working (现在分词)</td></tr><tr><td>过去将来</td><td>should would(原形)</td><td>should have + worked (过去分词)</td><td>should be + working (现在分词)</td><td>should have would been + working (现在分词)</td></tr></table>

注意：1. 一般现在时第三人称单数动词的形式，除了is（原形是be）和has（原形是have)以外，都是原形加s，规则同名词变复数，见第(十二)条。  
2. 动词的过去式和过去分词是原形加 ed, 但有些动词是不规则的; 动词的现在分词一律是原形加 ing。关于动词的变化见第(十六)条。

[2] 各种时态的用法：

1）一般现在时(the simple present tense)

① 动词的原形（be除外）就是一般现在时的形式，说的是当前存在的情况，或当前经常做的事情，或是永远不变的真理，如：

(a) It is cold today.  
今天天气冷。   
(b) We have six classes every day. 我们每天有六节课。   
(c) There are four seasons every year. 每年有四季。

② 遇到主语是第三人称单数时，除了have和be以外，都是在原形动词的词尾加s（规则同名词变复数），如：

He goes to school at seven every day in the morning.

他每天早晨七点钟上学。

③ have 和 be 这两个动词的变化是特殊的。have 的第三人称单数是 has; be (原形)的第三人称单数是 is, 另外还有只用于 I 的 am 和用于其它主语的 are。例如:

(a) I have a recorder. 我有录音机。   
(b) She has a television set. 她有电视机。   
(c) I am a teacher. 我是教师。   
(d) Her father is a doctor. 她的父亲是医生。  
(e) We are schoolmates. 我们是同学。   
(f) They are workers. 他们是工人。

2）一般过去时(the simple past tense),

①凡是已经发生过的事，如果只是说起了这回事，而与现在无关，就用一般过去时。一般说来，这种动词的形式是在原形动词的词尾加ed，规则见第(十六)条。例如：

I watched a performance last evening.  
昨晚我看了一场演出。

② 一般的过去式动词没有人称的变化，只有be是特殊的，am和is的过去式是was，are的过去式是were，如：

(a) I was at home yesterday evening.

昨晚我在家。

(b) They were at home yesterday evening. 昨晚他们在家。   
(c) I met him yesterday.  
昨天我遇到了他。   
(d) He met Tom yesterday.  
昨天他遇到了汤姆。

3）一般将来时(the simple future tense)：

一般将来时是从现在的角度来说，以后将怎么样。动词的形式是在原形动词前加助动词shall/will，第一人称(We/I)用shall，其它人称都用will，不分人称都用will也可以，还可以把助动词缩写为“'ll”和主语连接，如：I'll/He'll/…等。举例如下：

(1) We shall(will)meet tomorrow.

$$
= \text {W e} ^ {\prime} \text {I l m e e t t o m o r r o w}.
$$

我们明天见。

$②$ They will come soon.

$$
= \text {T h e y} ^ {\prime} \text {l l c o m e s o o n}.
$$

他们不久就要来。

③ It will snow.

$$
= \text {I t} ^ {\prime} \text {l l s n o w .}
$$

天要下雪。

4）过去将来时(the past future tense)：

过去将来时是指过去所说的将要发生的事，实际上还是过去的事。这种时态只需要在原形动词前加助动词 would 即可。若是分人称（一般可以不分），就把一般将来时的 shall 变为 should、will 变为 would。

should/would都可以和主语连接，简化为“‘d”，如：we'd/they'd/…等。举例如下：

$①$ I told him yesterday that I'd (I should/ would) go with him. 昨天我告诉他了我要和他一起去。

$②$ He said that he'd(hewould)come.他说他要来的。

5）现在完成时（the present perfect tense）：

这种时态说的是已经做过的事，但其影响还在，或此事还在继续。这种时态的动词总是用过去分词，只有助动词 have 遇到主语是第三人称单数时变为 has。have 和 has 可以与主语连接缩写成've 和's。例如：

$①$ I've(have)studied English for five years. 我已经学了五年英语了。（还在继续）

$②$ He's(has)studied English for five years, too. 他也学了五年英语了。（还在继续）

$③$ I've(have)readthisbook. 我看过这本书。（印象还在）

6）过去完成时(the past perfect tense)

过去完成时也可以说是过去的过去。这种时态说的是过去某时或某一行动之前已经发生过的事，一般要有时间状语。这种时态的动词形式是：助动词had（可以与主语连接缩写成'd）+过去分词。例如：

$①$ He'd (had) studied the plan before he began to work.

他在开始工作之前，已经对计划做过了研究。

② When I came in, he'd (had) just finished his

hework.

我进来的时候，他刚做完了作业。

7）将来完成时（the future perfect tense）：

这种时态是用来说明将来的某一时间之前将已完成的事，一般要有时间状语。这种时态的动词形式是：shall/will(可以与主语连接缩写为"i")have + 过去分词。例如：

By the end of January, we'll (shall/will) have finished this term.

到一月底，我们这一学期就已经结束了。

8）过去将来完成时（the past future perfect tense），这种时态是用来追述过去，预计过去未来的某时之前将已完成的事，一般要有时间状语。这种时态的动词形式是：should/would（可以与主语连接缩写为‘d）have+过去分词。例如：

He said that he'd (would) have worked for two years by the end of that year.

他说，到那年的年底他将已工作了两年了。

（that year指的是过去的某一年）

$②$ I told him that I'd (would/should) have left there before he returned.

我告诉了他，在他回来之前，我将已离开那里。

9）现在进行时（the present continuous tense）：

现在进行时动词的组成是：助动词am/is/are（可以与主语连接缩写为'm/'s/'re）+现在分词，am/is/are要随着主语变化，现在分词是固定不变的。这种时态表示的是此时此刻正在做什么，或当前这段时间里正

在进行的事，也可以用来表示准备要做的事，有时也可以加上 just/now/…这类状语。举例如下：

① We're (are) studying for the modernization of our country.

我们在为我们国家的现代化而学习。（这段时间正在做）

$②$ She's (is)studying.她正在学习。（说话时正在做）

$③$ I'm（am）writing a letter.我正在写信。（说话时正在做）

$④$ He's (is) reading the newspaper now. 他现在正在看报。（说话时正在做）

$⑤$ We're(are)just havinga class.我们恰好在上课。（说话时正在做）

$⑥$ I'm（am）just telling you about this.我正要把这事告诉你。（准备要做的事）

10）过去进行时（the past continuous tense）：这种时态用来说明在过去的某一时刻或某种行为发生的同时，正在进行着的事，一般要有时间状语。这种时态的动词形式是：was/were（随主语变化）+现在分词。例如：

① When he came yesterday, I was thinking about a plan.

昨天，他来的时候，我正在考虑一项计划。

② We were discussing some problems at that time.

那时，我们正在讨论一些问题。

11）将来进行时(the future continuous tense)：

这种时态用来说明从现在起，到将来某一时刻或某种行为发生之时，将一直在做着的事，一般要有时间状语。这种时态的动词形式是：shall/will（可以与主语连接缩写为'll)be + 现在分词。例如：

① We'll (shall/will) be waiting till you come. 我们将一直等到你来。   
② They'll (will) be having their class at the moment of your arrival.

在你到达的时候，他们可能在上课。

这种时态在口语中，常常用来代替一般将来时，如：

When will you be coming?

= When will you come?

12）过去将来进行时（the past future continuous tense）：

这是从过去的角度来说明在那时以后的某一段时间将要做着的事。这种时态的动词形式是：would/should（可以与主语连接缩写为'd）be+现在分词，常常是用在宾语从句中。例如：

I said one month ago that we'd(would/should) be expecting their arrival the next week.

一个月以前我说过，我们将在那时以后的下一个星期等待着他们的到来。

13）现在完成进行时（the present perfect continuous tense）：

这种时态的动词形式是：have/has(随主语变化，可

以与主语连接缩写为've/'s)been + 现在分词，说明早已开始，以后还要继续做着的事。例如：

① We've(have)been discussing the problem this half an hour.

我们对这个问题已经讨论了半个小时了。（还要讨论下去）

She's (has) been doing her homework for two hours.

她已经做了两个小时的作业了。（说话时还在做）

14）过去完成进行时（the past perfect continuous tense）;

说明开始的时间是在过去的某时之前，到过去的某一时刻为止一直在做着的事，一般要有时间状语。

这种时态的动词形式是：had（可以与主语连接缩写为'd)been + 现在分词。例如：

We'd (had) been preparing our lessons before the college-entrance-exam began.

在大学入学考试开始之前，我们一直在准备功课。

15）将来完成进行时（the future perfect continuous tense）;

这种时态表示的是在说话之前已经开始，到说话以后的某时之前一直在做着的事。这种动词的形式是：will/shall(可以与主语连接缩写为'll) have been + 现在分词。例如：

① Zhang Hong will have been studying at the university for four months by the end of this year.

到今年年底，张宏将已在大学学习了四个月了。

$②$ Before the meeting begins at ten tomorrow morning, we'll (shall/will) have been preparing for it.

在明天上午十点钟开会以前，我们将一直在为它做准备。

16）过去将来完成进行时（the past future perfect continuous tens);

这种时态表示的是，从过去的角度来说，到将来的什么时间（这种将来还是属于过去的范围）一直继续着的事。这种动词的形式是：would/should（可以与主语连接缩写为'd)have been + 现在分词，一般要有时间状语。例如：

He said that he'd (would) have been working there for ten years by the end of 1968.

他说，到1968年底，他将已在那里工作了十年了。（1968年是已经过去的一年）

# 附注：

1. 一般现在时的特殊用法：

（1）对于剧情或各种表演以及其它如在目前的情景的描述，常常是用一般现在时，如：

When the curtain rises, Juliet is sitting at the desk. The phone rings. She picks it up and listens quietly. Meanwhile the window opens and a masked man enters the room.

幕升起时，朱荷叶正坐在桌边。电话铃响了。她拿起

电话, 静静地听着。就在这个时候, 窗户打开了, 一个带面具的人进了屋子。

(2) 计划安排好了的事, 或说明确定无疑的事, 可以用一般现在时代替将来时, 如:

① We leave London at 10:00 a.m. next Tuesday and arrive in Paris at 1:00 o'clock. We spend two hours in Paris and leave again at 3:00. We arrive in Rome at 7:30, spend four hours in Rome.

下星期二上午十点钟，从伦敦启程。一点钟到达巴黎，停留两小时。三点钟再启程。七点半钟到达罗马，停留四小时。（某旅行社的一项预告）

$②$ Tomorrow is Sunday.

明天是星期天。（确切无疑）

2. 现在完成时, 一般不加说明时间的状语。但可以有以下几种情况的时间状语:

(1) 还未过去的一段时间, 如 this morning (今天早晨)/this afternoon (今天下午)/this winter (今冬)/today (今天)/…等。试看下列例句:

$①$ I haven't seen him this morning.

今天早晨我一直还未见到他。（说话时还在早晨）

② It has been cold this winter.

今年冬天一直是很冷的。（说话时还在冬天）

(2) 说明时间有多久, 用介词 for 加时间; 说明从过去的什么时候开始, 到说话时一直继续着的事, 用 since 做介词加说明什么时候的名词, 或用 since 做联词引导一个从句。例如:

① We have lived here for many years.

我们在这里住了多年了。（说话时还住在这里）

He has smoked since he left school.

他离开学校以后就吸起烟来了。（现在还吸）

③ She has been here since six o'clock.

她从六点钟就一直在这里。（现在还在）

(3) 现在完成时还可以加上一些非确定性的时间状语, 如:

$①$ He has just come in.

他刚刚进来。

$②$ They have always been busy.

他们一直在忙。

$③$ I have never seen the sea.

我从未见过大海。

(4) He hasn't come back yet.

他还未回来。

$⑤$ He has come back already.

他已经回来了。

⑥ Is everything ready yet?

一切都已准备好了吗？

Have you ever been there?

你到过那里没有？

3. 一般过去时和现在完成时的区别主要是看和现在有无

系。试把下列句子加以对比：

(1) He has lived there for two years.

他已经在那里住了两个星期（见书里）

(2) He lived here.

他在这里住过两个月。（现在已经不住在这里了）

(3) He has been ill for ten days.

他病了十天了。（现在还未好）

(4) He was ill for ten days.

他病了十天。（现在已经好了）

(5) She has been in bed for a week but now she is getting up.

她卧床休息了一周，现在可以起来了。（现在还在卧床）

4. 过去完成时所表示的都是在一般过去时之前的事。这种时态要加时间状语，或用于复合句中，或者是有可以说明是过去以前的事的上下文配合。例如：

(1) When I came in, he had already left.

我进来的时候，他已经走了。

(2) He suddenly realized that he had left his wallet in the bus.

忽然间，他想起来，他把钱包丢在公共汽车上了。

(3) George was eighty when our story begins. He had lived in the valley all his life.

当我们的故事开始时，乔治是八十岁。他已经在那个山谷里住了一辈子。

5. 过去进行时一般要有时间状语，说明是在过去的什么时刻。但遇到有前后文配合，足以说明是什么时刻时，也可时间状语，如：

a village. It was getting darker.

天黑起来了。

(2) Smoke

chimney of the

farmhouse. The farmer's children were playing with the dog and the farmer himself was leaning on his gate. I crossed the road and touched him on the elbow. "What do you want?" he said.

农舍的烟囱在冒着烟。农民的孩子们在逗着狗玩耍。农民自己靠在门边。我穿街走过去，碰了一下他的胳膊肘。他说：“你要干什么？”

6. 现在进行时和过去进行时还可以用来代替一般现在时和一般过去时，说明经常发生的事，如：

(1) He is continually losing his spacctacles. 他连续地丢眼镜。（现在经常发生的事）

(2) I was always losing my key. 我过去总是丢钥匙。（过去常有的事）

(3) She was talking to the secretary yesterday. 昨天, 他又找书记谈话了。(说明他常找书记谈话)

7. 有些动词或助动词可以与主语连接缩写，如 am—'m/ is—'s/are—'re/have—'ve/has—'s/shall (will)—'ll/should(would)—'d/had—'d/…等。

# (三十九)

# 虚拟语气

虚拟语气是想象，祝愿、让步或希望；

动词使用反常规， 只用过去和原形。

想象现在用过去， were用在各人称；

过去完成指过去， 其它相应变化同[2]。

祝愿、希望和让步，动词一律用原形3。

# 说明：

[1] 总的来说，虚拟语气（the subjunctive mood）不是陈述事实的。这种语气表示的是：① 纯粹的想象，② 美好的祝愿，③ 可能不是事实的让步状语，④ 希望能够做到的事情。在表达这些含义的句子中，动词的时态不按正常的用法，只用原形和过去时的各种形式。

[2] 纯粹的想象, 现在的事要用一般过去时动词, 动词 be 不分人称, 一律用 were; 过去的事要用过去完成时动词; 将来的事要用过去将来时动词; 过去将来的事要用过去将来完成时动词。另外, 在表示将来的从句中, 不管是第几人称, 都是在原形动词前加 should。试看下列例句:

1）现在的事：

① If I had a dictionary, it would help me much.

要是我有一本字典，那对我会有很大帮助。（事实上没有）

② If I were you, I would go.

我要是你，我会去的。（事实上不可能）

2）过去的事：

If you had come yesterday, you would have met her.

昨天，你要是来了，你会见到她的。（事实上没有来，也未见到她。）

3）将来的事：

If tomorrow should be fine, we would start.

明天，天气要是好，我们就动身。（估计天气不会好，事实上不可能动身。）

[3] 表示祝愿/希望被采纳的建议/可能不是事实的让步状语/ $\cdots$ 等，一律要用原形动词，如：

1）表示祝愿：

Good luck be yours!

祝你顺利！

2）表示希望被采纳的建议：

I propose that he be excused.

我建议对他给予宽恕。

3）表示可能不是事实的让步状语：

Though he abuse me, I will not be angry.

（可能不是事实） （陈述事实）

尽管他骂我，我也不会生气。

# 附注：

1. 虚拟和陈述事实可以混合使用, 如:

1) It is time we left. (事实) (虚拟)

该是我们走的时候了。(It is time说的是事实；we left说的是该走，但事实上没有走。)

2) I wish I were you. (事实) (虚拟)

但愿我是你。（wish是事实，但“我是你”是不可能的虚拟。）

2. would (had) rather(sooner) 后加一般过去时从句，可以用来表示将来或现在不可能实现的希望，如：

1) I would rather they came tomorrow. 我倒愿意他们明天来。

2) I would sooner you did it now. 我倒愿意你现在就做。

# 练习(39)

说明下列虚拟语气句的种类和所指的时间：

① If he were to ask you, what would you say?   
If he had not helped you, would you have failed?   
③ If she should not come tomorrow, what would you do?   
(4) Success be to you!   
⑤ Though it rain, I will go.   
$⑥$ I hope that my proposal be adopted.   
⑦ Someone bring him a glass of water.   
$⑧$ I would help you if I were able.

# 附录

# I. 加注阅读材料

(1)

It is often noticed that a pneumatic tire which is only moderately firm in the morning, when the bicycle or automobile is first taken upon the road, may be much harder by noon, as if more air had been put into it. The same thing will occur if the machine is allowed to stand in the sun. The additional pressure may, indeed, become so great as to burst the tire. Of course it is very clear that no air has been added to that which was in the tire in the morning, for if the rubber will retain the air which is in the tire, it will be equally effective in preventing more from entering.

(O. W, Caldwell and W. L. Eikenberry, Elements of General Science)

# 注释：

① 此句可以译为：“常常地看到，早晨刚一上路时只是中等硬度的自行车或汽车车胎，到了中午硬度就更大了，好

象气体增多了似的。”句子开头的 It 是形式主语，从句 that a pneumatic tire may be much harder by noon 才是真正的主语，which is only moderately firm in the morning 又是修饰 that…从句的主语 a pneumatic tire 的定语从句，when the bicycle or automobile is first taken upon the road 和 as if more air had been put into it 都是从句的状语从句。因为是说明一种客观存在的现象，动词都用一般现在时。as if more air had been put into it 这个从句中的 had been put 是虚拟语气动词，相当于一般现在时。

② 在科技文章中，常常是用“will+原形动词”来说明会产生的结果，是“就会…”的意思。这一句可以译为：“如果把车辆置于阳光的照射下，同样的情况就会发生。”

③ 此句可以译为：“很明显，车胎内的气体是和早晨那个时候一样的，并没有增加，因为能够保住气体的车胎同样地也会防止气体的进入。”此句的it是形式主语，真正的主语是从句that no air has been added to that which was in the tire in the morning. which was in the tire in the morning 是主语从句中that 的定语从句。for if…from entering 是推断性原因状语从句, if the rubber will retain the air which is in the tire 又是这个状语从句中的状语从句，which is in the tire 又是if the rubber…从句中air的定语从句。

# (2)

Young animals are strikingly like children in their craving for amusement. A young bear will lie on his

back and play with his feet and toes by the hour①, while a young puppy can have a great game② with only a dry bone, or by chasing his shadow on the wall. Rabbits come out in evenings on the sand-hills to play hide-and-seek with their young, and squirrels never weary of this universally popular game. I know a young fox that used to come from an adjacent wood every evening to play with a young fox-terrier. They became great friends③ and were often seen in the woods together.

(Royal Dixon, The Human Side of Animals)

# 注释：

$①$ by the hour论小时地，以小时来计算地。  
$②$ haveagreatgame做一场兴致勃勃的游戏。  
③ great friends 真正的好朋友。

# (3)

It is high noon. There is stillness in the air that impresses you, broken only by the low murmur of the brook behind and the ceaseless song of the grasshopper among the weeds in front①. A tired bumblebee hums past, rolls lazily over a clover blossom at your feet, and has② his midday luncheon. Under the maples near the river's bend stands a group of horses, their heads touching. In the brook below are the patient cattle, with patches of sunlight gilding and bronzing their

backs and sides. Every now and then $③$ a breath of cool air starts out of some shaded retreat $④$ , plays around your forehead, and passes on. All nature rests $⑤$ . It is her noontime.

(F. Hopkinson Smith, A Day at Laguerre's)

# 注释：

① 此句可以译为：“气氛给人以沉寂之感，冲破这种沉寂的只有背后那条小溪的潺潺流水声和前面草丛中不断的虫鸣声。”句中的 that impresses you 是 stillness 的定语从句；broken …in front 是分词词组，也是 stillness 的定语。

$②$ has吃。  
③ every now and then 不时地。  
④ starts out of some shaded retreat 从阴凉处刮出来。  
⑤ All nature rests 一切都是静悄悄的。

# (4)

This was my first sight of the California country landscape①, and I saw it at the most beautiful time of the year. The low-rolling hills② were bright green③, against which blended the darker green of the park-like oaks④. Over the slopes were washes of color where the wild flowers grew⑤, like bright scarves laid out in the sun. They were of deep orange, or an equally deep purple, or, perhaps, of mingled white and purple. Each variety, and there were many of

them, seemed to grow by itself so that the colors were massed.

(Stewart Edward White, Gold)

# 注释：

① the California country landscape 加利福尼亚的乡村景色。  
② the low-rolling hills 豌蜒起伏的山峦。   
$③$ brightgreen鲜绿色的。  
$④$ against which blended the darker green of the park-like oaks is a non限定性定语从句，联词 which 前加了介词 against，这个从句的意思是：映衬着园林似的橡树的墨绿色。   
⑤ washes of color泾渭分明的彩色涂层。  
$⑥$ seemed to grow by itself 好象是各自成片地生长。

# (5)

Success grows out of struggles to overcome difficulties. If there were no difficulties, there would be no success①. If there were nothing to struggle or compete for, there would be nothing achieved②. It is well, therefore, that men should be under the necessity of exerting themselves. In this necessity for exertion we find the chief source of all human advancement—the advancement of individuals as of nations③. It has led to most of the splendid mechanical inventions and improvements of the age. It has stimulated the ship

builder, the merchant, the manufacturer, the machinist, the tradesman, the skilled workman. In all departments of productive industry, it has been the moving power. It has developed the resources of this and other countries—the resources of the soil, and the character and qualities of the men who dwell upon it. It seems to be absolutely necessary for the purpose of stimulating the growth and culture of every individual. It is deeply rooted in man, leading him ever to seek after, and endeavor to realize, something better and higher than he has yet attained.

(Samuel Smiles, Thrift)

# 注释：

① 虚拟语气，可以译为：“要是没有困难，也就不会有成功了。”  
② 虚拟语气，可以译为：“要是无所为，就将无所得。”  
③ the advancement of individuals as of nations 个人的也是民族的进步。   
$④$ the moving power动力。   
⑤ the character and qualities of the men who dwell upon it 可以译为：“居住在这块土地上的那些人们的性格和品质。”who dwell upon it 是 the men 的定语从句。  
⑥ man指的是人类而不是具体的一个人。  
⑦ yet已经。

# (6)

It is curious to note how ant societies resemble and differ from those of man. Human societies may be divided into six classes or stages—the hunting, pastoral, agricultural, commercial, industrial and intellectual; and ants have stages corresponding to the first three. Some ants live solely by the products of the chase<sup>1</sup>; they are known as<sup>2</sup> the driver and legionary ants. Some keep domestic animals, in the shape of plant lice, scale insects and caterpillars<sup>3</sup>; these belong to the pastoral class. The agricultural class is represented by the harvesting ants, which collect, store, and it is said, plant seeds<sup>4</sup>. Against these resemblances may be set the fact that ant societies are almost solely composed of females<sup>5</sup>, for the males take little part in the social life of the colony<sup>6</sup>. Each female is predestined to a certain task, and an ant community may be likened to a big family. A very large family it is in some cases<sup>7</sup>, for Forel has estimated that a community may consist of five hundred thousand ants. Such a community resembles a perfect republic<sup>8</sup>, where each works for the good of the whole community, each having her appointed work, laboring constantly for the good of all and each ready to sacrifice herself for the good of all. It is a veritable insect Utopia<sup>9</sup>.

(C. A. Ealand, Animal Ingenuity of To-day)

# 注释：

① Some ants live solely by the products of the chase. 可以译为：“有些蚂蚁专靠猎取为生”。  
② they are known as 它们被认为是。   
③ Some keep domestic animals, in the shape of plant lice, scale insects and caterpillars 可以译为: “有些蚂蚁从事于作为家畜的黏虫、甲虫和毛毛虫的饲养。”   
④ and it is said, plant seeds 可以译为：“据说还能种植”。   
⑤ Against these resemblances may be set the fact that ant societies are almost solely composed of females, … 可以译为: “蚂蚁社会几乎只是由雌性组成的这个事实, 可以看做是与这些相似之处的不同之处”。这是一个倒装句, 正常的顺序应为: The fact that ant societies are almost solely composed of females may be set against these resemblances。   
⑥ colony群落。  
⑦ may be likened to可以比做。   
⑧ in some cases 按照某些情况来看。   
a perfect republic 1   
Utopia乌托邦(可望而不可及的理想国)。

# (7)

When the early settlers camped beside the rural stream, they got water from the stream, built their own fire<sup>①</sup>, and supplied and cooked their own food. Thus they provided for practically all their needs<sup>②</sup>. In the

communities with which we are familiar one group of workers produces and distributes food materials; another group looks after the water supply; another looks after coal or other materials for heating the homes; another gathers and disposes of garbage and other wastes; another cares for health regulations by seeing that water and food are kept reasonably clean; another watches to see that fire is not harmful. Clearly our modern life is much more complex than was that for the family of early settlers, who made their home for the night beside the stream. It should prove valuable and interesting to study some of the ways in which modern science has enabled men to meet these increasing problems of the life of our own times.

(O. W. Caldwell and W. H. D. Meier, Open Doors to Science)

# 注释：

$①$ built their own fire生起火来。   
② Thus they provided for practically all their needs 因而保证了实际生活的需要。   
③ food materials 食物原料。  
$④$ Clearly our modern life…beside the stream. 全句可以译为：“显然，现代生活，比起早期移民的那种家庭生活来，要复杂得多了，早期的移民是以河边为家来过夜的。”注意：这句话中的动词时态有一般现在时也有一般过去时, than前说的是现代的生活，用一般现在时, than后说的

是过去早期移民的生活，用一般过去时。than后的wasthatforthefamilyofearlysettlers是thatforthe familyofearlysettlerswas的倒装形式。who…beside the stream是一个非限定性定语从句，who指的是early settlers。

⑤ It should prove...of our own times 句中的 It 是形式主语, 真正的主语是 to study...of our own times. should prove valuable and interesting 中的 prove 后省去了 to be, 意即: 当可证明, ...是有价值的、是引人入胜的。

# (8)

No man or woman who has been an idler or a shirker has ever received the homage of others. The faces that we go to the art museum to study, the faces that we look at a second time on the streets①, are those of men and women who have accomplished difficult things, who have been the hardest workers. For the spirit that makes men work eagerly and gladly brings strength and beauty to their faces. A man who once rode in a locomotive with an aged engineer② said that in the most tense moments of the swift night journey through snowdrifts and in the face of biting winds, there was a "radiance shining through the wrinkles of the engineer's face that almost made the darkness light about him③." It was the joy of doing a hard task well that made the engineer's face radiant amidst soot, noise, darkness,

and storm. When the faces of our workers become sullen and weary, then America's future will be in peril④.

(Grace A. Turkington, Community Civics)

# 注释：

① the faces that we look at a second time on the streets 中 的 that we look at a second time on the streets 是 the faces 的定语从句，意即：那些我们在街上看到过的脸型。  
$②$ aged engineer上了年纪的火车司机。   
$③$ made the darkness light about him 使他的周围在黑暗中发光。   
$④$ in peril处于危机之中。

# (9)

Cats are gifted① linguists. By mewing they can just as plainly express a desire to have a door opened or closed② as if they requested it in so many words③. A friend has furnished me④ an interesting account⑤ of her cat's ability to make herself understood⑥. It seems that the cat, with three small kittens, at one time⑦ slept in a box prepared for her in the kitchen. But one night when it was particularly cold, some one left the kitchen window open⑧, and late in the night the cat went to her mistress's bed and mewed continuously until her mistress arose and went to the kitchen and closed the window. The cat was perfectly satisfied⑨, as she

had made her great need understood®.

(Royal Dixon, The Human Side of Animals)

# 注释：

① gifted 天生来的,具有天赋的。  
② to have a door opened or closed 让人把门打开或关上。   
③ as if they requested in so many words, 虚拟语气, 动词requested相当于request, 意即; 好象是他们用很多的话来提出要求似的。   
$④$ A friend has furnished me 一位朋友曾经给我讲述过。   
⑤ an interesting account 一件有趣的事。   
⑥ to make herself understood 让别人明白她的意思。  
⑦ at one time 曾经。  
⑧ left the kitchen window open 没有关厨房的窗户。  
The cat was perfectly satisfied 那只猫十分地满意了。   
⑩ as she had made her great need understood 因为她已经让人懂得了她的迫切需要。

# (10)

Once, in the winter, many years ago, when I had been cutting holes through the ice in order to catch pickerel①, as I stepped ashore I tossed my axe back on to the ice, but, as if some evil genius had directed it②, it slid four or five rods directly into one of the holes, where the water was twenty-five feet deep. Out of cu

riosity③, I lay down on the ice and looked through the hole, until I saw the axe a little④ on one side, standing on its head, with its helve erect and gently swaying to and fro with the pulse of the pond; and there it might have stood erect and swaying⑥ till in the course of time⑦ the handle rotted off, if I had not disturbed it. Making another hole directly over it with an ice chisel which I had, and cutting down the longest birch which I could find in the neighborhood with my knife, I made a slip-noose, which I attached to its end, and letting it down carefully, passed it over the knob of the handle, and drew it by a line along the birch, and so pulled the axe out again.

(Henry David Thoreau, Walden)

# 注释：

① When…to catchickerel 是个时间状语从句，句中的 had been cutting…是过去完成进行时动词，意思是：一直不停地…  
② as if…had directed it, 虚拟语气从句，过去完成时 had directed 相当于一般过去时 directed，意思是：好象是鬼使神差似的。   
③ out of curiosity 出于好奇。  
④ a litte 一点点。until I saw the axe a little on one side 意即：直到我看见斧子的一点侧影。  
⑤ swaying to and fro with the pulse of the pond随着池水的荡漾而前后摇摆。

⑥ and there it might have stood erect and swaying…表达的是一种推想，谓语用的是情态动词might加完成时不定式，意即：它可能会竖立在那里不停地摇摆…  
⑦ in the course of time 经过一定的时间。  
$⑧$ rottedoff烂掉。  
⑨ If I had not dirturbed it, 虚拟语气, 过去完成时 had not disturbed 相当于一般过去时 did not disturb, 说明并非事实的假设, 意思是: 要是我不去管它的话 (实际上是管了)。   
Making…I had, and cutting down…with my knife 中的 Making…和 cutting down…是两个分词词组做状语，它们的逻辑主语是 I。  
⑪ which I attached to its end 是 slip-noose 的非限定性定语从句, 意思是: 把它 (指 slip-noose 套索) 拴在桦树枝的一头。  
$\mathbf{12}$ …, passed it over the knob of the handle, and drew it by a line along the birch, and so pulled the axe out again 中的 passed 前省去了 I, passed 与前边的 made 是平行的, 主语都是 I。letting it down carefully 是分词词组做 passed…的状语, 后边的 drew 和 pulled 也都是与 made 并列的谓语动词。此句的意思是: 小心在意地把套索放下去, 套住斧柄, 搀动附在桦树枝上的拉线, 这样就把斧子又给拉出来了。

# (11)

No boy can afford to neglect his work, and with a boy work, as a rule, means study. Of course there

are occasionally brilliant successes in life where the man has been worthless as a student when a boy. To take these exceptions as examples would be as unsafe as it would be to advocate blindness because some blind men have won undying honor by triumphing over their physical infirmity and accomplishing great results in the world. I am no advocate of senseless and excessive craming in studies, but a boy should work, and should work hard, at his lessons—in the first place, for the sake of what he will learn, and in the next place, for the sake of the effect upon his own character of resolutely settling down to learn it. Shiftlessness, slackness, indifference in studying, are almost certain to mean inability to get on in other walks of life. Of course, as a boy grows older, it is a good thing if he can shape his studies in the direction toward which he has a natural bent; but whether he can do this or not, he must put his whole heart into them. I do not believe in mischief-doing in school hours, or in the kind of animal spirits that results in making bad scholars; and I believe that those boys who take part in rough, hard play outside of school will not find any need for horseplay in school. While they study they should study just as hard as they play football in a match game. It is wise to obey the homely old adage, “Work while you work; play while you play.”

(Theodore Roosevelt, The Strenuous Life)

# 注释：

① can afford 经得起。   
$②$ with a boy 对一个男孩来说。as a rule, means study 按照常理，指的就是学习。   
③ Of course…when a boy 这一句的大意是：当然，偶尔也有学童时期并不起眼而后来成了大事的人。in life 一生中。as a student 作为一个学生。when a boy 是 when he was a boy 的省略，是 where 从句的状语从句；因为这个从句的主语 he 指的就是它所附属的句子中的主语 the man，这个从句的谓语动词又是 was，故主语和谓语动词都可以省略。  
$④$ advocate提倡。  
⑤ blindness 稀里糊涂。  
⑥ no advocate of 不赞成。  
⑦ in studies 在学习上。  
to get on other walks of life 从事于别的工作。  
$⑨$ natural bent 自然的趋向。  
put his whole heart into them 专心一致地去做。   
⑪ believe in 相信。  
② animal spirit 活跃好动。  
③ results in 造成…的结果。  
$④$ making bad scholars 学习不好。  
$⑤$ horseplay 恶作剧。

# (12)

The animal that Ichabod① bestrode was a broken-

down② plow-horse③, that had outlived almost everything but its viciousness. He was gaunt and shagged, with a ewe neck, and a head like a hammer; his rusty mane and tail were tangled and knotted with burs; one eye had lost its pupil, and was glaring and spectral, but the other had the gleam of a genuine devil in it④. Still he must have had fire⑤ and mettle⑥ in his day⑦, if we may judge from⑧ the name he bore of Gunpowder⑨. He had, in fact, been a favorite steed of his master's, the choleric Van Ripper⑩, who was a furious rider, and had infused, very probably, some of his own spirit into the animal; for, old and broken-down as he looked, there was more of the lurking devil in him⑪ than in any young silly in the country.

(Washington Irving, The Legend of Sleepy Hollow)

# 注释：

① Ichabod 是一个人的名字，可以译为“艾查巴德”。  
$②$ broken-down衰弱的。  
③ plow-horse 耕地拉犁的马。  
$④$ had the gleam of a genuine devil in it 闪着凶光.   
$⑤$ fire火气。  
⑥ mettle烈性。   
⑦ in his day 在他年轻的时代。  
⑧ judge from 从…来判断。   
the name he bore is the name which he bore 的简略,

省去了联词 which，意思是：他取得的名字。

the name he bore of Gunpowder 可以译为：“他取得的‘火药’这个名字”。

⑩ the choleric Van Ripper 性格暴燥的万·里勃。万·里勃是该马原来主人的名字。

⑪ in him 在他的身上。

# II. 书写标点

# 1. 大写(Capitalization):

(1) 每一句的第一个字母要大写, 如:

The report, so far as I am concerned, is false.

(2) 直接引语每一句的第一个字母要大写，如：

She said, "You may go when you have finished the task."

（3）诗歌每一行的第一个字母都要用大写，如：

Country Scene, South of the Yangtze River  
As we homeward paddled in one another's com  
pany,  
To the ferry when 'twas getting dark,  
Fallen flowers seemed to long for our society,  
Lingeringly following our bark.

注：①此诗是储光羲的“江南曲”，原诗为：“日暮长江里，相邀归渡头。落花如有意，来去逐船流。”

② '!was = it was.

（4）代词I不论是否在句首都要用大写，如：

However late you arrive, $\underline{1}$ will wait for you.

(5) 专用名词的第一个字母要大写, 如 Canada/George/Mount Rainier/Lake Superior/…等。

注意：

① 专用名词由几个词组成时，每个词的第一个字母一般都要大写，但其中的虚词可以不用大写，如 the Declaration of Independence/the Jefferson High School/Alexander the Great/…等。  
$②$ 专用名词后边加通用名词构成专用名词时，通用名词的第一个字母一般是用大写，但也可以小写，如：the Colorado River (river)/Beihai Park (park)/…等。  
③ 通用名词前的专用名词只起定语作用时，通用名词不用大写，如European history/the Danish people/…等。

（6）周日、月份和节日名称的第一个字母总是要大写，如Saturday/November/National Day/…等。  
（7）方向指的是地区时，第一个字母要大写，如：He was born in the South.   
(8) 通用名词作为称呼时, 第一个字母要大写, 如 Uncle Harry/Dr. Sullivan/Mr. Peterson/Miss Anna/ Mrs. Brown/…等。  
(9) 书刊名称和文章标题第一个词和所有实词的第一个字母都要大写, 如 Nature/The Rime of the Ancient Mariner/Biology and Human Life/…等。

2. 斜体字 (Italics) 一书刊名称、拉丁文以及其它外来语可以用斜体字书写，如 Literary Digest/Treasure Island/in situ/in vitro/…等。

3. 标点(Punctuation):

（1）句点（Period）：

1）加在陈述句和祈使句的句末，如：

$①$ Vacation will soon be here.   
$②$ Pay close attention to what I say.

2）加在缩写词后，如 $\mathbf{Y}_{-}\mathbf{M}_{-}\mathbf{C}_{-}\mathbf{A}_{-} / \mathbf{No}_{-} / \mathbf{etc}_{-} / \mathbf{Sept}_{-} / \dots$ 等。  
3）加在编号数字后，如I.Materials and Methods/1.The Process of Cardiac Depolarization/…等。  
4）加在与正文连接的小标题后，如 Estuary back-water./Lemma 9./\*等。

注意：

① 与正文连接的小标题可以只大写第一个字的第一个字母，题后加句点。  
② 不与正文连接、单独做一行的小标题不加句点。

(2）问号(QuestionMark):

1）加在疑问句后，如：

① Where do you live?   
② Do you not believe me?

2）加在有疑问的陈述句后，如：

You are surprised?

3）用括号加在有疑问的词后，如：

In 1587(?) Shakespeare went from Stratford to London.

注意：直接引语疑问句变为间接引语后，要加句点，不能加问号，如：

He asked me where I lived.

(3）惊叹号（Exclamation Mark)加在感叹句或表示惊讶、高兴、厌恶、祝愿的词、词组或其它句子之后，如：

1) How glad I was to be at home again!   
2) That boy a senior! Impossible!   
3) Wish you happy!   
4) Why are you late!   
5) Hurrah!   
6) Cold as hell!

(4) 逗号(Comma):

1）加在称呼之后，如：

Owen, you may recite.

2）作为补充说明的同位语要用逗号与句中的其它部分隔开，如：

① Julius, our janitor, has lived an interesting life.   
$②$ Sodium bicarbonate, or baking soda, has many uses.

注意：起限定作用的、必不可少的同位语不要加逗号，如：

(a) The word knave has an interesting history.   
(b) The expression I'll tell the world is slang.

3）书写年月日时，在日期后加逗号，如：April 30, 1978; 书写地址时，在小地名后加逗号，如: Seattle, Washington; 人名附加称号时，在称号前加逗号，如: Charles Briggs, Jr.

4）句首的状语或独立成分后要加逗号，句中的插入语或补充说明一般要用逗号与其它部分隔开，如：

(1) Certainly, I will do.   
② Long long ago, there existed a castle on the top of the mountain.   
$③$ He was not convinced, however, by what I said.   
Miss Annes was, indeed, an excellent teacher.   
My old friend, being obliged to work his way through college, had no time for athletics.

注意：句首的状语如果是一个词或简短的词组而且在表意上是必不可少的，后边可以不加逗号，如：

On New Year's Night the whistles were blown and the bells were rung.

5）并列的词或句要用逗号分开，如：

① Most of the tickets have been sold, but there are still a few good seats left.   
$②$ He often has bread, milk, cheese and eggs for breakfast.   
$③$ He is a jovial, generous, even-tempered man.

注意：

A. 并列词有连词连接时, 可以不加逗号, 如:

(a) Philip and Charles are cousins.   
(b) I met not only him but his wife also.

B. 有三个以上的并列词时，只在最后一个词前加连词，如：

Are you a farmer, a worker or a scholar?

C. 并列词有时也可以只用逗号隔开而不加连词, 如例句③。

6）直接引语与主句之间要加逗号，如：

① "I was sent to meet you," he said.   
$②$ He asked, "When did they arrive?"   
③ “Where,” he asked, “will you go?”   
$④$ "If you go," replied Albert, "you go at your own risk."

注意：

① 直接引语每句第一个字的第一个字母总是要大写，如以上各句。  
② 主句如果在直接引语后，第一个字的第一个字母不要大写，如例句①③④。  
$③$ 主句加在直接引语中间时，主句前的引语部分后面和主句之后都要加逗号，如例句 $③④$   
④ 主句前的直接引语，除了可以加感叹号或问号外，即便是完整的句子也只能加逗号，如例句①。

7）逗号可以用来表示有省略词，如：

One of my brothers is a lawyer; the other,

an actor. (other 后省略了 is)

(5）分号(Semicolon)：

1）比较复杂的并列句要用分号分开，如：

① It was no affair of mine, I thought; besides, it was difficult to know what to do.

$②$ Preliminarily, it can be related to: (i)relatively high elevations with which the basis were initially formed, and incomplete compensation due to their width; (ii) surface manifestation of denser lithospheric slab subducted under some basins; (iii) uplift of the lithosphere by compressional stress in the deep mantle.

2）句后加上用namely（viz.）/that is (i.e.)/forexample (e.g.)/…等引导的作进一步说明和举例的句子时，前面要加分号，如：

He was a very courteous yet absent-minded man; for instance, I once-heard him apolo-gize to a desk for having bumped against it. 注意：如namely等这类词后不是句子而是词或词组时，前边加逗号也可以，如：

Sentences are of four kinds, namely, declarative, imperative, interrogative and exclamatory.

(6) 冒号 (Colon) 一加在后边带有列举或说明的词句之

后, 如:

1) Mrs. Wendell, president of the club, spoke as follows: "It gives me great pleasure..."

2) There are, in general, two kinds of sport writing. (i) the reporting of contest, and (ii) discussion of various conditions in the athletic world:

3) An interview is a report of a conversation between a public man and a reporter: it is usually the man's answers to a series of questions asked by the reporter.

4）加在正式书信中的称呼后，如Dear Dr. B. G. Unni:/Dear Sirs:/…等。

(7) 破折号(Dash)一长度相当于两个联词号的横线, 用于:

1）话语的突转，如：

Yesterday,I met one of your friends,a Mr. -what was the man's name?

2）总结概括，如：

Light, air, food, heat, and moisture—these are the five essentials of life.

3）补充说明，如：

Frances is exactly my age—fifteen.

4）插入句子中间的同位语，前后可加破折号，如：

Her most cherished possessions—her book, her flowers, and her pets—were the only companions she desired in her old age

5）说明从…到…，如30-60minutes/20-30 degrees/…等。

（8）圆括号(Parentheses)：

1）用于附加的补充说明，如：

① What explanation(if any) can you offer?   
② Then he began to make excuses (I had expected that he would), but I remained firm in my demands.

注意：

① 附加在句中括号内的词、句，除遇有缩写点外，末尾可以不加标点；但中间要加上必要的标点。如：

a. … (books, magazines etc.)…   
b. …with some food and beer (partly bought, partly stolen)…

② 不属于句中的括号内附加说明，第一个字母一律要大写、末尾应加句点，简单的词或词组也可以不加。如：

a The doctor, coach, and principal stood near the injured player. (Three persons, clearly distinguished by their titles.)   
b. Robert said that he should go with me. (Indirect statement)

2）编号可以放在圆括号内，注意括号外不加任何标点，如：（1）Choice of supporting electrolytes/（4）Effects of $\mathsf{pH} / \dots$ 等。

(9) 方括号(Brackets):

1）遇到圆括号中还需要加括号时，可以用方括号，如(seeFigs.8-18of[14])。有时也会出现圆括号内再加圆括号的情况，如：（see（b)above）。

2）给别人的作品加补充或说明时，用方括号，如：In the year 1734 [actually 1733] the first edition of the book was published.

(10) 引号(Quotation Marks):

1）直接引语的前后加引号，如：

"How well you look!" exclaimed her mother. 注意：

$①$ 如引号中还需要用引号时，可用单引号 $(\dots)$ 如：

"Yes," said Anne, "when I told her that, she replied 'You are mistaken.'

$②$ 引用分段的原文时，在每段的开头加引号，在最后一段的后边加引号，如：

The full text of his letter reads as follows:

"Mr. G. H. Wetmore of your office told me recently that...

"As to my character and fitness for the position...

If you wish to see me, I shall be glad to…

2）特定的名称加引号，如 the“Gold-digger”。

(11）省字号(Apostrophe[加在上角的逗号])：

1）用来代替省掉的字母，如 won't/I'm/it's/…等。  
2）加在s的左上角表示数字、字母和指的是哪一个词的复数，如p's/q's/7's 9's/if's/…等。

(12) 联词号 (Hyphen) 是长度相当于一个字母的短横线, 用来连接合成词, 如: self-made/bad-tempered/…等。  
(13) 删节号(Points)可以用来表示词句的删节, 如: There was general agreement that the speaker… had chosen his subject wisely.

注意：删节号一般是三个点或六个点。删节号后遇有句点可以省去。

(14) 星号(Asterisk $[\ast ]$ ) 可以用来标在需要加注解的词句的右上角, 如: Lenôtre* laid out the gardens at Versailles.

# III. 信柬格式

# 1. 书信 (Letter):

（1）内容式样(Parts of a letter)如下：

![](a10103e7f4f53fd1dbf0ec2b31ac2f8d96afe9f003f3bb41253d4b594f439d4d.jpg)

说明：

① 信头(The heading)一发信人的地址和发信日

期。

$②$ 信内姓名、地址（The inside address）——收信人的姓名和地址。

③ 称呼(The salutation)——对收信人的称呼，熟人可以用简称，如Dear Philip；生人用全称，如Dear Mr. Philip Draper;如果是对单位，又不知收信人姓名时，可以写Dear Sirs/Dear Gentlemen/…等。称呼后加冒号（:）或逗号（,）都可以。

④ 信文(The letter proper)——同一般文章的写法。

⑤ 致意(The greeting)——信文后另起一行写With best regards!/With highest esteem!/…等，相当于中文信的“问好!”/“敬礼!”/…等。注意第一个字母要大写，后加惊叹号。

⑥ 结尾(The conclusion)——在右下方第一行写 Truly yours, (对不认识的人)/Sincerely yours, (对认识的朋友)/Affectionately yours, (对亲戚或家人)/…等, 相当于中文信结尾的“敬启”/ “启”/“谨启”/…等(注意: 后边要加逗号(,)，开头的字母大写。yours也可以放在前面, 写成 Yours truly, /Yours sincerely, /Yours affectionately, /…等; 第二行是发信人签字; 第三行是发信人的工笔或打字全名(熟人可以不写)。如写给素不相识的人, 工笔全名前还可以加上 Miss/Mr./Mrs. /…等; 第四行是发信人的职务, 个人信件不写。

⑦ 附及(The postscript)——对信文还要加以补充

时，可在信后加附及，标明P.S.(Postscript的缩写)，下面写附加内容，如：

P.S.

Herewith are the proofs for you to read.

(2）信封(Envelope）一右上角为贴邮票处，左上角为发信人的姓名和地址，右下角为收信人的姓名和地址。样式如下：

Mr. Johnny Wild

Wadsworth Pen Company

486 Mission Boulevard

Los Angeles, California

stamp

Mr. Philip Draper

587 Clarendon Avenue

Springfield, Massachusetts

附注：

1）如由某人收转，可在收信人的名字下加上 $\mathfrak{c} / \mathfrak{o}\times \times \times$ 如：

Mr. Philip Draper

c/oMrs.PaulScott

Rural Route 7, Box 184

Mortonville, Georgia

2）有些需要标明的字样，可以加在信封的左方，如：

① If not delivered, please return. (无法投递请退回)   
$②$ Personal或Private(亲启或手拆）  
③ Confidential（机密）

(4) Please Forward! (请转本人)   
⑤ Introducing Mr. $\times \times \times$ （介绍 $\times \times \times$ [由被介绍人面交]）  
⑥ kindness of Mr. $\times \times \times$ （烦 $\times \times x$ 带交）  
⑦ Immediately(要件)   
⑧ Urgent(急件)  
⑨ Rush(快件)   
10 Registered 或 R（挂号）  
$\mathbb{1}$ Express Delivery(快信）  
⑫ By Air Mail 或 Par Avion（航空）  
③ Printed Matter (印刷品)   
14 Manuscripts (稿件)

2. 请柬(Invitation)一用第三人称的口气说明谁邀请谁，在什么时间参加什么活动，最后在左下方写明地点和发柬日期。以下是请柬和回柬的写法举例：

(1) 发出请柬(Writing of invitation),

Mr. and Mrs. Douglas Forbes Lamont request the pleasure of Mr. Edward Burleson's company at dinner on Wednesday evening, October the twenty-fourth, at seven o'clock.

87 Kirkland Road

October the sixteenth

(2) 回柬接受邀请 (Reply for accepting an invitation);

Mr. Edward Burleson accepts with pleasure Mr. and Mrs. Douglas Forbes Lamont's invitation to dinner on Wednesday evening, October the

twenty-fourth, at seven o'clock.

416 Burlington Avenue

October the seventeenth

(3) 回柬谢绝邀请 (Reply for declining an invitation):

Mr. Edward Burleson regrets that he cannot accept Mr, and Mrs. Douglas Forbes Lamont's invitation to dinner on Wednesday evening, October the twenty-fourth.

416 Burlington Avenue

October the seventeenth

# 后记

此书所能起到的作用，只不过是把头绪纷纭的问题，根据实用的需要，集中概括起来。歌诀归纳的是最基本的规律，附注对有关细节及特殊情况加以补充。希望它对学习英语者能够有所帮助，也可以供应用者之参考。

# 补遗

1. 有时数词也可以象名词一样变为复数，但只限于用在 of 加名词之前的概数，如 several hundreds of guests 几百位来宾 / tens of thousands of tourists 好几万旅游者 /…等。直接加在名词前说明具体数量的数词没有复数，如 five hundred (thousand/million/billion) lbs. 五百（千/百万/十亿）磅。

2. 原形动词前加助动词 do/does/did，后边不加 not 时，起到的是加强肯定的作用，如：

I did see him.

我确实见到了他。

（以上分别作为第（十二）条和第（二十七）条附注之补充。）
